 kings 11 ne ballebaaji ke alaava gendbaaji main bhi behtareen pradarshan kiya he

 hawaii kiraaya bachaane ke idia se shuru hua unka bijness aaj karodon kaa turn over paar kar chukaa he
 How the business started: Nishant Pitti and Rickant Pitti's father had to travel a lot as a businessman
 zyaadaatar samay kisi trevell agent kii madad se hi tikat book karaayaa jaataa tha
 But one day when Rikant saw that the travel agent was taking 1000-1500 rupees more on every ticket, then he realized the loss

 ek din main unhen lagbhag 10-15 tikat book karnaa padataa tha

 ab har tikat par kuch paise unhone charge karne shuru kar die

 mil gaya maukajab bahut zyada tikat kii booking ek hi ypi adress se hone lagi to ek company ne unhen notice karnaa shuru kiya aurtravel partnerbanane kaa ofer bhi diya
 The company also agreed to give an incentive amount of six per cent

com

 isse purvadilli hoicourtne chunaav ayog kii sifarish or raashtrapati kii adhisuchana ko radd kar diya tha

 However, the Commission rejected the petition filed by the mlas on May 16 to allow the cross-examination of the petitioner on this basis
 isamen vidhayakon ne patel ke alaava dilli vidhansabha or dilli sarkaar ke un adhikariyon se alag-alag jirah karne kii ijaajat maangi thi, jinhone tamaam sabooton ke aadhaar par vidhayakon dwaara bataur sansadeey sachiv sarkari kharch par kaam karne or vittiya laabh lene kii baat kahi thi

 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Delhi's shopkeepers have come out on the road carrying bread and placards in their hands against the Rent Act
 unka kahana he ki dilli main bhi gujarat rajya kii tarah rent act lagu kiya jaae
 In fact, turban shopkeepers in Gujarat enjoy equal status as owners
 haalanki beete varsh aae supreme court ke order ne dilli rent control act ko jaij tehraaya tha, lekin in logon kaa kahana he ki sarkaar chaahe to act main sanshodhan karke gujarat kii tarj par dilli main bhi act bana sakati he
 These shopkeepers had long ago taken over the turban from the owners by paying some price to the shops
 kuch dukandaar to aise hai jinhone kareeb 50 saal pehle pagadi dekar dukaan kiraye par lee thi
 Those people are now refusing to give these shops back to the landlords
 aatmadah kii di dhamkee, raashtrapati se lagaayenge guhaarpradarshan kar rahe logon kaa kaha he ki agar unki maange nahin maanin gayi to ye log aatmadah karne ko majaboor ho jaaenge or raashtrapati se ichhamrityu kii guhaar lagaayenge
 Leader of Opposition in Delhi Legislative Assembly Vijender Gupta has made many allegations against the Kejriwal government regarding the metro
 unhone kaha ki aam aadmi party kii sarkaar ne dilli metro ke chauthe charan kii sweekruti kii filon ko aktubar 2014 se, atirikt metro coach kharidne kii file june 2016 se tathaa dilli-meerut rapid rail trogit system kii file disambar 2016 se rokkar rakhi he
 Vijender Gupta said that the Kejriwal government wants to stall the pace of development in Delhi by conspiring to hang these metro projects
 unhone kaha ki somvaar ko vah is maamle ko dilli vidhansabha main uthaaenge
 The BJP leader said that the Kejriwal government is not only suppressing the files of approval for the fourth phase of Delhi but is also deliberately delaying the decision to purchase additional coaches in the Delhi Metro
 sarkaar ke kehane par dilli metro ne june 2016 main 916 or kochon ko kharidne ke liye vistrut pariyojna report bheji thi, parantu dilli sarkaar ne iskaa koi uttar nahin diya
 Delhi Metro sent a proposal for the purchase of 582 coaches in January 2017, reducing the number of coaches to be purchased
 yah prastaav bhi dilli sarkaar ke paas lambit he
